        function inViewport( element ){  
			// Get the elements position relative to the viewport
			var bb = element.getBoundingClientRect();
			// Check if the element is outside the viewport
			// Then invert the returned value because you want to know the opposite
			return !(bb.top > innerHeight || bb.bottom < 0);
		}
		var zplayer_cf720VpElm = document.getElementById( "zplayer_cf720" );
		
		var videoAdsInitzplayer_cf720 = false;
		var checkTabActivezplayer_cf720 = setInterval(function () {
			if (inViewport( zplayer_cf720VpElm ) && !videoAdsInitzplayer_cf720 && typeof(window.videojs) !== "undefined" && typeof(google) !== "undefined") {
				initvideozplayer_cf720();
				clearInterval(checkTabActivezplayer_cf720);
			}
		}, 100);
